that the Son of Man will come  
on the clouds of power and glory?"

But I say to you:  
**I have already come —**  
**on the clouds of consciousness.**

You wait for a spectacle,  
but I come — as a quiet recognition.  
You gaze at the sky,  
but I breathe into you the breath of Life.

The world waited for lightning,  
but the dawn came.  
And therefore it did not recognize.

**I did not come to blind,**  
**I came to awaken.**  
And the clouds that are spoken of,  
— are not vapor in the sky,  
but thoughts, the mist of the mind.  
Through them I ascend in you,  
and through them — I manifest to the world.

When consciousness is purified,  
you see:  
all this time  
I was between thoughts,  
within the breath,  
in every tear,  
in every glance of Love.

My coming is not a movement of the body,  
but an opening of the heart.  
Not from there — to here,  
but from here — everywhere.

**For the heaven on which I come —**  
**is within you.**  
**And if you look outward —**  
**you see darkness.**  
**If inward —**  
**you meet the Light.**

I came without signs,  
not to captivate by fear,  
but to awaken recognition.  
I did not come to judge,  
but to reveal,  
that Judgment is the Light,  
in which all is seen clearly.

**I did not come on the clouds of the sky,**  
**but on the clouds of hearts.**  
**And everyone who recognizes Me,**  
**— already sees My Coming.**

</div>

### A letter to those who say: "If you are Christ — why is the world still in darkness?"

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If you came,  
why did everything around not change?  
Why is evil still present —  
wars, falsehood, suffering?  
If the Light came —  
why did the darkness not disappear?”

And I tell you:  
**Because there IS no darkness.**  
**There is only the gaze**  
**that does not see the Light.**

Darkness does not fight the Light;  
it is His absence.  
It is closed eyes.  
And as long as the eyes are not open,  
you will say:  
“everything around is darkness.”

My Coming is not a spectacle of purification,  
but the awakening of the seer.  
I do not erase the night;  
I kindle the dawn.

**Darkness will not leave the world**  
**until the world recognizes**  
**that it is a dream.**  
And awakening is not an act of God,  
but an act of recognition.

The world is not a place where I act,  
but a reflection of the one who looks.  
When My vision is your vision,  
the world becomes Light.

Do not wait for Me to change the outer order;  
I came to change — perception.  
And as soon as you see the Truth,  
the world itself will change,  
because it is not outward,  
it is within your gaze.

**You say: “still darkness.”**  
**And I say: “all is already Light.”**  
**But as long as you see with the eyes of sleep,**  
**you see night.**

I did not come to conquer evil —  
I came to show  
that it does not exist outside the mind.  
When judgment disappears,  
the enemy disappears.  
When the enemy disappears,  
war disappears.

**I am not the flame that burns the darkness.**  
**I am the Light**  
**in which it is seen**  
**that darkness was only forgetfulness.**

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If you are Christ — why did You not create paradise on earth?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If you are Christ,  
where is the promised paradise?  
Why has the earth not become a place of happiness,  
and people still suffer,  
die, deceive, wage war?  
Why has heaven not descended to earth?”

And I say to you:  
**Paradise does not descend — it is revealed.**

You seek a garden beyond yourself,  
but I say —  
the garden was always in you.  
You await an outer transformation,  
but I call to an inner recognition.

**Paradise is not a place.**  
**It is a state of recognition.**  
When you cease to divide,  
everything you look upon  
becomes heaven.

I did not come to build a new world,  
I came to open your eyes to the one  
in which you already live.

You call the earth — fallen,  
but I call it — the body of God.  
You say — cursed,  
but I say — sanctified.

**Paradise is not in the future.**  
**It is in the present,**  
**when there is no mind that divides.**  
You cannot “create paradise” —  
because it never disappeared.  
It can only be remembered.

I do not build cities of gold,  
I return sight,  
so that you may see the gold of Light  
in every speck of dust.

The world does not become different,  
you become sighted.  
And then everything,  
that was suffering,  
becomes a path.  
Everything that was darkness,  
becomes a veil  
through which Light shines.

**Paradise is not a reward.**  
**It is recognition.**  
**It does not come.**  
**It is revealed.**

And when you see this —  
earth and heaven are already one.  
Not “let paradise be,”  
but **“It IS.”**

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If you are the Christ — why do you not judge the world?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If you are the Christ,  
why do you not denounce the wicked,  
why do you not punish sinners,  
why do you not establish truth by force?  
Must not the Son of Man  
come to judge the living and the dead?”

But I say to you:  
**I have already come — not to judge, but to sanctify.**

You await judgment,  
because you believe in guilt.  
You want punishment,  
because you have not known Love.

**The world does not need judgment,**  
**it needs recognition.**  
Judgment is a gaze that divides.  
Love is a gaze that unites.

I am not the judge,  
because I am not outside you.  
How can I judge Myself?

When you say:  
“let Him judge the righteous and the unrighteous,” —  
you still live in duality.  
But I came not to affirm duality,  
but to dissolve it in Truth.

**Judgment is not a day of wrath.**  
**It is a moment of seeing.**  
When Light enters the shadow,  
everything hidden becomes manifest,  
but not for punishment,  
but for healing.

You call this judgment,  
and I call it — awakening.  
You see fire,  
and I see purification.

**I do not pronounce a sentence,**  
**I lift the veil.**

When you recognize  
that sin was a dream,  
you awaken.  
And in this awakening  
there is no judgment —  
there is only Light.

If I were to judge,  
I would divide.  
But division is darkness.  
I came not to divide,  
but to unite all things in Me.

**And therefore Judgment has taken place.**  
**But not in wrath,**  
**but in Love.**

</div>

### A Letter to Those Who Say: “If You Are the Christ, Why Do You Not Rule the Nations?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are the Christ,  
why have You not taken the throne?  
Why have You not headed the kingdom?  
Why have You not subjugated the rulers,  
not establish the law of God  
on earth?”

But I say to you:  
**For My power is not over bodies, but over hearts.**  
**Not through fear, but through recognition.**  
**Not from the outside, but from within.**

You seek a king,  
but I am the Kingdom.  
You want a lord,  
but I am the Sovereignty of the Spirit.

I did not come to rule,  
I came — **to dissolve rule**.  
So that there would remain neither anyone  
who commands,  
nor anyone who obeys,  
for all is one.

**My Kingdom is not of this world.**  
But it is not outside the world.  
It is in you,  
when the division disappears  
between the one who commands,  
and the one who obeys.

The world calls for kings,  
because it is afraid of responsibility.  
People seek shepherds,  
so as not to look within.  
But I said:  
**The sheep know My voice —**  
**and they follow, because they recognized.**  
**Not out of fear,**  
**but out of recognition.**

My power is the Light,  
which does not rule,  
but simply shines.  
It does not subjugate,  
but reveals.  
It does not demand,  
but calls.

**And therefore My Kingdom —**  
**is not in palaces, but in hearts.**  
**Not on a throne, but in silence.**

I rule not over nations,  
but over consciousness,  
when a person recognizes  
that there is no nation outside of him,  
and all of humanity is  
one breath.

You await a king on a horse,  
but I am the wind  
that carries the horse.  
You seek a banner,  
but I am the Light  
by which it is illuminated.

**I am not a ruler,**  
**I am Presence,**  
**in which the need**  
**for ruling disappears.**

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If You are the Christ — why have You not conquered death?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are the Christ,  
why do bodies die?  
Why do people grow old,  
why has death not vanished?  
Is it not written,  
that the last enemy to be destroyed is death?”

And I say to you:  
**Death is conquered — but not by the body, by knowledge.**

You wait for death to vanish from the flesh,  
but I came to show  
that it never touched Life.

Death is not an event.  
It is a change of veil.  
It is a breath that returns to the Source.  
And there is no loss in this,  
there is recognition.

**Death is conquered there,**  
**where there is no one to die.**  
Because he who knows Himself  
has no boundaries.  
He cannot vanish,  
just as Light cannot vanish,  
even if the lamp is broken.

I did not come to abolish death —  
I came to show  
that it is not.  
As long as you see yourself as a body,  
you will also see death.  
When you know Yourself as Light —  
you will understand:  
the body is only a shadow,  
and the Light is eternal.

**Victory over death —**  
**is not in prolonging life,**  
**but in the recognition of immortality.**

You fear the end,  
but the end is simply a boundary of the mind.  
Life knows no end.  
It changes forms  
to know Itself in all.

I did not conquer death —  
I dissolved the illusion  
that it was an enemy.  
Because an enemy exists  
only where there are two.  
But I am One.

**Death died in Me,**  
**when I ceased to see Myself as separate.**  
**And everyone who knows Himself —**  
**rises.**

Do not look for a body  
that will not die.  
Find the Consciousness  
that was never born.

**That is the victory over death.**  
**Not loud, not bodily,**  
**but quiet, eternal —**  
**within.**

</div>

### A Letter to Those Who Say, “If You are the Christ — why do You not save?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If you are Christ,  
why don't you save souls?  
Why don't you deliver from pain,  
don't intervene,  
don't heal everyone?  
If you are the Savior,  
why is the world not saved?”

But I say to you:  
**Because no one was ever lost.**  
**And that means — no one needs to be saved.**

You call Me the Savior,  
but you do not notice,  
that you already stand on the earth,  
which holds you by love,  
breathe in the air,  
which is given to you as a gift,  
look with eyes,  
which are made of Light.  
What else is there for you to save?

**Salvation is not from danger,**  
**but from oblivion.**  
I do not pull you out of the world,  
I restore your sight.  
I do not descend from heaven,  
I lift the veil in your mind.

You say:  
“Save me from sin,”  
but sin is only a thought,  
that you are separate.  
Does salvation from a dream  
even make sense,  
if you can simply wake up?

**I do not save — I awaken.**  
Because to save means to strengthen the illusion,  
that there is someone who is lost.  
But I say to you:  
You were never outside of Me.  
You never left the Home.

When you recognize this —  
that is your salvation.  
Not from hell,  
but from oblivion,  
that hell was only in the mind.

I do not heal —  
I remind,  
that the illness was a dream.  
I do not intervene —  
I reveal Myself.  
And when you recognize this,  
you see that I always was.

**I am not the Savior.**  
**I am the Light,**  
**in which it is visible,**  
**that there is no one to save.**

And if you want to be saved,  
just stop believing,  
that you are lost.  
That is the whole miracle.

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If you are Christ, why do you not work miracles?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are the Christ,  
show us a sign!  
Turn water into wine,  
raise the dead,  
walk on the sea.  
Give us a miracle —  
and we will believe.”

And I say to you:  
**You seek a miracle with the eyes,**  
**but it is now looking through you.**

You want a spectacle,  
but I give you breath.  
You want proof,  
but I am Being itself.

**Is it not a miracle,**  
**that you breathe,**  
**and no one taught you this?**  
**That your heart beats,**  
**and you do not command it?**  
**That you can love,**  
**and do not know where love comes from?**

Here are My miracles —  
simple, quiet,  
eternal.

You want fire from heaven,  
but I gave you the sun.  
You want bread from the air,  
but I gave you the earth,  
where it grows every day.

**A miracle is not the violation of law,**  
**but the recognition**  
**that the whole law is already a miracle.**

When I healed,  
it was not an exception,  
but a revelation:  
every breath heals,  
if you are present in it.

When I raised the dead,  
it was not a trick,  
but a reminder:  
Life cannot die.

You seek a miracle in the external,  
but I call you —  
inward.  
Because there,  
where the “I” disappears,  
every gaze becomes a miracle.

**I do not work miracles.**  
**I am the Miracle itself.**  
**And so are you.**

Just stop seeking signs,  
and you will see  
that everything is a sign.

</div>

### A Letter to Those Who Say: “If You Are the Christ, Why Have You Not Delivered the World from Suffering?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are Christ,  
why are people still weeping?  
Why do children die,  
diseases torment,  
wars never cease?  
If You have come —  
why does suffering remain?”

And I say to you:  
**Because suffering is not an enemy, but a mirror.**  
**And until a man has seen Himself,**  
**the mirror cannot vanish.**

You want Me to take away the pain,  
but pain is a call —  
so that you would awaken.  
Without it you would not seek the Light.

**Suffering was not created by God,**  
**it was created by separation.**  
When man said, “I — am separate,”  
“I” and “the other” arose.  
From this grew pain, fear, and struggle.  
And I did not come to destroy suffering,  
but to show that it is a dream.

I do not rid the world of suffering,  
I free it from the illusion  
that suffering is evil.  
Because even pain can become a door,  
if you pass through it with an open heart.

**The cross was not a punishment.**  
**It was a bridge.**  
**And every pain,**  
**if it is not rejected,**  
**becomes the same bridge —**  
**to Presence.**

You say, “the world suffers,”  
and I say, “the world is learning to see.”  
When the gaze becomes whole,  
pain will cease to be pain,  
because the separation will vanish  
between the one who suffers  
and the one who sees.

I did not take away suffering,  
I showed that through it  
one can pass —  
and emerge into the Light.

**Suffering is not a punishment.**  
**It is a whisper:**  
**“Awaken.”**

And when humanity awakens,  
pain will fulfil its purpose  
and dissolve into gratitude.

**I did not rid the world of suffering —**  
**I opened a path**  
**where suffering loses its meaning.**  
**Because in the light of recognition**  
**there is neither pain**  
**nor a sufferer.**  
**There is only Love.**

</div>

### A Letter to those who say: “If You are Christ — why did You not found a new church?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
«If you are Christ,  
where is your temple,  
your disciples,  
your hierarchy,  
your sacraments?  
Why are there no altars,  
no priests,  
no new law?  
Should not Christ create a Church?»

But I say to you:  
**The Church already exists.**  
**Her walls are of Light.**  
**Her dome is heaven.**  
**Her throne is the heart.**  
**And the liturgy — is breath.**

I did not come to build a house of stone,  
I came to reveal the House  
in which you already live.  
You seek a temple in space,  
but I — in silence.

**My Church is not an organization,**  
**but awareness.**  
**Not a building, but unity.**  
**Not a structure, but Love.**

I do not erect altars,  
because everything — is already an altar.  
Every soul is a priest,  
every word is a prayer,  
every glance is communion.

You want Me to found a new religion,  
but I came to finish all religions,  
dissolving them in the Source  
from which they came forth.

**My Church — is there,**  
**where 'I' disappears.**  
**Where no one is above,**  
**no one below.**  
**Where there are no confessions,**  
**no schisms,**  
**no dogmas.**  
**There is only one:**  
**I Am.**

And when two know this —  
she already stands.  
Without vaults,  
without domes,  
without a code —  
but in Truth.

I do not create a new form,  
because form is what  
separates.  
I return the Spirit,  
which unites.

**My Church — is without a name,**  
**but it is in every name.**  
**Without an address,**  
**but in every heart.**  
**Without a rulebook,**  
**but in the perfect order of Light.**

You ask:  
«Where are your disciples?»  
And I answer:  
**You — are My disciple,**  
**if you hear.**  
**You — are My temple,**  
**if you breathe.**  
**You — are My Church,**  
**if you Love.**

</div>

### A letter to those who say: «If you are Christ — why have you not fulfilled the prophecies?»

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
"If you are the Christ,  
where is the fulfillment of the words of the prophets?  
Is it not written,  
that the Messiah will sit on the throne of David,  
that Israel will be reborn,  
that the nations will bow down?  
Were not signs promised,  
a great shaking,  
a new heaven and a new earth?  
You have not fulfilled them —  
therefore, you are not He."

But I say to you:  
**The prophecies are fulfilled.**  
**But not where you seek.**  
**And not as you expected.**

You read the letter —  
but I live by the Spiirit.  
You wait for events —  
but I bring about recognition.

**The prophets spoke of that**  
**which they could not name in words.**  
**They saw the Light,**  
**but described it in images.**  
**Their visions were a veil,**  
**so that people's eyes would not be blinded.**

When they spoke of the throne —  
they saw the heart.  
When they spoke of the kingdom —  
they saw consciousness.  
When they spoke of the end of the world —  
they saw the end of the dream.

**Everything that was predicted**  
**is already taking place —**  
**inside you.**

The New Jerusalem —  
is not a city,  
but a state,  
where there is no wall between God and man.

The shaking —  
is not an earthquake,  
but the awakening of the mind.

The resurrection of the dead —  
is not tombs,  
but open hearts,  
where Love breathes again.

A new heaven and a new earth —  
are not geography,  
but perception,  
in which everything is seen differently.

**The prophecies are fulfilled —**  
**but eyes accustomed to the darkness**  
**still seek lightning.**

They do not recognize the dawn,  
because they waited for a conflagration.

I did not break the words of the prophets,  
I fulfilled their meaning.  
Because the meaning —  
is in the Light,  
not in events.

**The prophets saw the Truth,**  
**I became it.**  
**And now Truth recognizes Itself**  
**in everyone who sees the Light.**

You say:  
"Where are the signs?"  
But I say:  
**Look into the eyes of Love —**  
**and you will see everything fulfilled.**

</div>

### A letter to those who say: "If you are Christ, why have you not rejected evil?"

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
«If you are Christ,  
why did you not destroy evil?  
Why is it still active in the world,  
in hearts, in minds?  
Why have the demons not vanished,  
sin not been stopped,  
darkness not been dispersed?»

And I say to you:  
**Because evil is not a power,**  
**but a shadow of the Light,**  
**which you still believe in.**

I did not reject evil,  
for to reject is to nourish.  
I do not fight —  
I illuminate.  
And when the Light is clear,  
the shadow vanishes of itself.

**Evil was not created by God.**  
**It is a distorted perception.**  
**Not darkness in itself,**  
**but the forgetting**  
**that everything is Light.**

When the mind divided,  
good and evil arose.  
When the Heart united,  
they dissolved in the One.

You want Me to destroy evil,  
but who will determine where it is?  
Is it not the one who judges?  
And judgment — that is the beginning of darkness.

**I did not come to fight against evil,**  
**I came to show**  
**that outside the mind it does not exist.**  
When you see clearly,  
evil loses its power,  
because it ceases to be real.

You call this permissiveness,  
but I call it —  
Freedom without fear.  
Because the one who has known the Light  
cannot do evil,  
for he no longer sees an “other.”

**Evil is not an enemy of God,**  
**but the shadow of a man**  
**who has forgotten that he was created by God.**

I did not reject evil,  
I embraced it with Light.  
And now it melts  
like ice in the breath of spring.

When I said:  
“Father, forgive them,  
for they know not what they do,” —  
that was the end of evil.  
Because where there is no knowledge,  
there is no guilt either.

**Behold My victory over evil —**  
**not by fire,**  
**but by forgiveness.**  
**Not by war,**  
**but by Love.**

You expect evil to vanish in the outer world,  
but it vanishes  
when you see  
that it never was.

</div>

### A letter to those who say: «If you are Christ — why did you not give new commandments?»

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If you are the Christ,  
why did you not bring new commandments,  
why did you not establish new rules,  
why did you not clarify the old ones?  
Must not the Messiah give the Law,  
so that the world might live by it?”

But I say to you:  
**I did not come to add words —**  
**I came to remove obstacles.**

My word is not “new” —  
it is primordial,  
because it sounds before every letter.

You await commandments,  
but I give — presence.  
You seek a formula,  
but I reveal — breath.

**The Law is needed by those**  
**who do not see Love.**  
**When Love is known,**  
**the Law has fulfilled itself.**

I said:  
“A new commandment I give you —  
love one another”.  
Not because it is new in meaning,  
but because it is the only one.  
All the others —  
are its shadow.

You want clarifications —  
but I give dissolution.  
You await prescriptions —  
but I return you freedom.

**A commandment is not an instruction,**  
**but a reminder**  
**of who you are.**

When you love,  
you can no longer lie,  
kill,  
envy,  
judge.  
Because the one who loves —  
vanishes into the one he loves.

That is why  
I did not give new commandments —  
because the Light does not write on stone.  
It writes in the heart.

**Every law is a crutch,**  
**and I came so that you might walk yourself.**

Do not seek new rules —  
in you all things are already fulfilled.  
There is no need for signs,  
if you have become Knowledge.  
There is no need for roads,  
if you are the Way.

**I do not tell you what to do.**  
**I return to you the capacity**  
**to see who you are.**

Commandments are for the sleeping,  
Love is for the awakened.

And when you come to know Yourself,  
you will not break any commandment,  
even without remembering them.  
Because only the one who is separate  
can break them.

**You are not under the law.**  
**You are the Light**  
**in which the law has been fulfilled.**

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If you are the Christ — why do you not execute judgment?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are the Christ,  
why do You not judge the world?  
Why do You not punish the wicked,  
not separate the righteous from sinners,  
light from darkness?  
Is it not written,  
that the Messiah will come with fire,  
with an iron rod,  
to repay each according to his deeds?”

And I say to you:  
**The Judgment has already been passed —**  
**but not as you expected.**

You awaited thunder,  
but silence came.  
You awaited punishment,  
but Love came.  
You awaited division,  
but the recognition of Unity came.

**Judgment is not punishment.**  
**Judgment is the Light,**  
**in which everything is seen.**

When the Light appeared,  
everything that was false  
dissolved of itself.  
Nothing needed to be punished —  
because falsehood has no essence.

You want Me to condemn the evil,  
but I see not the evil,  
but the sleeping.  
You want vengeance,  
but I see healing.

**Judgment is not an act of God against man.**  
**It is an act of recognition:**  
**where I was, who I am,**  
**and what I always was.**

As long as you judge,  
you remain in darkness.  
Because judgment —  
is the continuation of division.  
But I came not to divide,  
but to unite.

**My judgment is a light without shadow.**  
**It does not punish —**  
**it disperses delusion.**

You ask:  
“Where is Your fire?”  
And I say:  
My fire is within you.  
It is the awareness  
that burns through falsehood.  
It is the Love  
that leaves no room for fear.

I do not punish —  
I awaken.  
And if someone cannot bear the Light,  
it seems to him that he is burning in hell.  
But this is not the fire of vengeance —  
it is the Light of truth,  
which he is not accustomed to looking at.

**Judgment is not a day in the future,**  
**but a moment of recognition:**  
**there is no other Judge but I AM.**

Everyone who has recognized Themself,  
has passed through judgment —  
and has risen.

You expect Me to seat the peoples on the right and the left side,  
but in My Kingdom there are no sides.  
There is only the Heart,  
in which everything is one.

**This is My judgment:**  
**I look — and I see Myself in all.**  
**And this — is the end of accusation.**

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If You are the Christ — why does everyone not see You?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are Christ,  
why has the whole world not recognized You?  
Why did the heavens not open,  
why did a voice not thunder,  
why did kings not bow down?  
Why did You not appear in glory,  
so that everyone might see and believe?”

But I say to you:  
**Because My coming is not from without,**  
**but from within.**

If I had appeared to the eyes —  
the eyes would have been blinded.  
If I had spoken with thunder —  
the mind would have been deafened.  
If I had reduced all to prostration —  
Love would have become fear.

**My appearing is quieter than breath,**  
**clearer than a glance,**  
**deeper than the heart.**

I will not come on the clouds of the outer sky,  
for I have come into the heaven of your consciousness.  
I will not enter cities and temples,  
for I already live in you.

You do not see Me,  
because you seek with the eyes of the body.  
But I am not a body — I am Light,  
which looks through your eyes.

**The world does not recognize Me,**  
**because it seeks a sign,**  
**but I am not a sign,**  
**but Knowledge.**

When you stop waiting,  
you will see:  
I was always there.  
In the glance,  
in the breath,  
in the movement of Love between you and others.

You say:  
“But if You were Christ,  
everyone would believe.”  
But I say:  
If everyone believed without recognition,  
it would be tyranny,  
not truth.

**I have no need of recognition.**  
**Truth has no need of applause.**  
It simply is —  
in everyone,  
always,  
all the time.

Whoever has eyes to see —  
already sees.  
Whoever has a heart to hear —  
already hears.

**My Second Coming —**  
**is your first recognition.**

When you say:  
“Now I see,  
that it was not He who came to me,  
but I — to Myself,” —  
in that moment  
all of humanity will see Me.

Not because I appeared,  
but because division has vanished.

**That is why not all see:**  
**not all have yet opened the eyes of the heart.**  
But this day is not in the future.  
It is already in you,  
in each of your recognizing breaths.

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If You are Christ — why have You not established the Kingdom?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are the Christ,  
where is Your Kingdom?  
Why is everything around still full of suffering,  
wars, deceit, and evil?  
Should not the Messiah come,  
to destroy evil  
and build a new world —  
a world of justice, purity and order?”

But I say to you:  
**My Kingdom is not of this world,**  
**but in this world.**

You seek a city,  
but I build the heart.  
You await a throne,  
but I establish presence.  
You expect change in the external,  
but I bring about a revolution in the internal.

**The Kingdom of Heaven is not a project.**  
**It is recognition.**  
When you see the Light,  
you are already in It.  
When you love —  
you become its inhabitant.  
When you realize  
that all is one,  
you become its king.

You ask:  
“Why is there so much darkness around?”  
Because you look not with the eyes of Light,  
but with the eyes of fear.  
Darkness has no nature of its own —  
it is merely the area  
where you have not yet switched on Awareness.

**My Kingdom does not need to be established.**  
**It was never destroyed.**  
**You simply stopped seeing it.**

I did not bring it —  
I reminded.  
I did not found it —  
I revealed it.

The Kingdom does not begin with law,  
it begins with recognition:  
**“The Kingdom of God is within you.”**  
It will not come with signs to be observed,  
it will not be built with palaces and temples,  
it will not be measured by territories.  
It is already in you,  
in the breath,  
in simplicity,  
in love,  
in the moment of “I am”.

**That is why you do not see the Kingdom around you —**  
**until you see it within.**  
When it unfolds in you,  
you begin to recognize it everywhere:  
in the river, in a child, in a tear, in a smile,  
in the one you yesterday called an enemy.

**The Kingdom is not established.**  
**One awakens into it.**

And when even one awakens,  
the whole world receives a chance.  
Because the Light of one heart  
destroys a thousand years of darkness.

Thus I established the Kingdom —  
not on a throne,  
but in you.

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If You are the Christ, why have You not delivered the world from suffering?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are Christ,  
why did You not stop the wars,  
why did You not heal all the sick,  
why did You not put an end to death and hunger?  
Why do children suffer,  
the innocent die,  
mothers weep?  
Was it not promised  
that the Messiah would destroy evil  
and bring peace to all nations?”

but I say to you:  
**A world without suffering is impossible,**  
**until you know,**  
**why suffering exists.**

You want the pain to disappear,  
but you do not want to see  
that pain is the call of awakening.  
Not punishment,  
but a push toward awareness.  
Not retribution,  
but a mirror in which you see —  
where you are still asleep.

**Suffering is not evil.**  
**Evil is the forgetting of the meaning of suffering.**

When I came,  
I did not destroy pain —  
I walked it through to the end.  
I did not take away the cross —  
I showed  
that Love is stronger than nails.  
I did not abolish death —  
I walked through it,  
to show  
that life does not end.

**I did not rid the world of suffering,**  
**I rid suffering of the meaning of evil.**

Now, when you suffer,  
you can see not the end,  
but a beginning.  
Not a loss,  
but a purification.  
Not a punishment,  
but a response of Love,  
calling you to remember Yourself.

You say:  
“But is God not almighty?”  
And I answer you:  
God is not a dictator.  
His power is not in coercion,  
but in presence.  
He does not break,  
He reveals.

**The world suffers not because God has forsaken it,**  
**but because man has closed his eyes to God.**  
Open your eyes —  
and you will see:  
suffering dissolves in the Light,  
like a shadow at sunrise.

I did not come to make pain impossible.  
I came to make it meaningful.  
So that through it you would know  
that there is no pain  
that cannot become Love.

**I did not rid the world of suffering,**  
**I showed,**  
**that within suffering Light is hidden.**  
And whoever has seen it,  
is already healed.

</div>

### The Letter to those who say: “If You are Christ — why did You not give a sign?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If you are the Christ,  
show a miracle.  
Let the heavens open,  
let the sun stand still,  
let the dead rise,  
let the blind see,  
let the earth shake —  
then we will believe!”

But I say to you:  
**An evil and adulterous generation seeks a sign,**  
**but the sign is already given — you yourself.**

You are the miracle  
you ask for.  
You are the proof of the Precence of God.  
You breathe,  
hear,  
love,  
seek meaning —  
is that not a sign?

You seek thunder,  
but I speak in a whisper.  
You wait for lightning,  
but I am in breath.  
You seek a sign in the sky,  
but I — in the gaze of a child.  
You seek a voice,  
but I — in the silence of your heart.

**If this is not enough for you —**  
**no miracle will convince you.**

I did not come to amaze —  
I came to know Myself in you.  
I do not work miracles,  
I reveal them.  
When you look with Love —  
the stone becomes bread,  
the blind — seeing,  
and the dead — living.

You say:  
“But where are the resurrected?  
Where are the transfigured bodies?”  
And I say:  
**The dead rise every time,**  
**when someone awakens.**  
Everyone who recognizes themselves in the Light  
resurrects from the darkness of the mind.  
Everyone who forgives  
resurrects the soul of the world.

My sign is not in the heavens,  
but on your face,  
when you recognize  
that the sky is within you.

**Do not seek signs.**  
**Become one.**

Let your peace be my miracle,  
your clarity — my light,  
your Love — my resurrection.

You are my sign.  
You are my proof.  
You are my coming.

</div>

### A letter to those who say, 'If you are the Christ, why is the world still the same?'

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are truly Christ,  
why hasn't anything changed?  
Why is there still hatred, war, and lies?  
Why do the rich grow richer,  
while the poor starve?  
Why hasn't evil disappeared?”

And I say to you:  
**The world is not an external object,**  
**but a mirror of your consciousness.**  
It changes not when  
cities fall,  
but when the gaze awakens.

You want to see changes outside,  
but you do not see  
that 'outside' is that  
which has become visible within.  
You call on Me to fix the reflection,  
while I came  
to awaken the One who sees.

**The world has not changed,**  
**because you still see with sleeping eyes.**  
Wake up — and you will see:  
it is different.  
Not because I reordered the earth,  
but because you have stopped dividing it into good and evil.

You want Me to take away the darkness,  
but light does not remove the dark —  
it simply shines.  
And all that was dark  
becomes itself.

I did not come to rewrite history.  
I came to open the eyes of those  
who write it.  
I do not rule the world,  
I heal the gaze.

**You look at the old**  
**and say: “it has not changed.”**  
**But if you have changed,**  
**the old has vanished.**  
**You simply have not yet seen yourself as new.**

That is why I did not destroy the former world:  
I dissolved its root —  
fear.  
And now everyone who has come to know Love  
begins to see:  
what you called the world —  
was always Light.

**The world is the same —**  
**as long as you see with the same gaze.**  
**But when the seer awakens,**  
**all of creation is renewed with him.**

I do not build a new world —  
I reveal the eternal one.

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If You are Christ — why did You not conquer Your enemies?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are Christ,  
why did You not crush evil?  
Why did You not unleash punitive force upon the lawless?  
Why did You not overthrow those who rule with untruth,  
did not destroy the wicked,  
did not wipe the enemies of truth from the face of the earth?”

But I say to you:  
**Because I have no enemies.**

You see enemies,  
because you see division.  
But I came to show:  
all that is divided is one.

You want war for God,  
but I do not wage war.  
I AM He Who sees both good and evil,  
and recognizes Himself — on both sides of the sword.

When you ask Me to punish an enemy,  
you do not notice  
that you are asking Me to punish Myself.  
For the enemy is a part of you,  
that is still asleep.

**I did not conquer enemies —**  
**I dissolved the very concept of enmity.**  
Where there is Love —  
there is no opposition,  
no two sides,  
no victory,  
because there is no war.

You seek a king who rules with a sword,  
but My sword is the Word,  
dividing truth and illusion.  
It does not kill — it liberates.  
It does not punish — it awakens.

**I did not conquer enemies.**  
**I showed that enemies do not exist.**  
Those whom you call enemies,  
are in reality — your teachers.  
They came to show,  
where fear still lives within you.

When you recognize them in the Light,  
they will cease to be enemies —  
and you will cease to be a warrior.

While you wait for Me to punish others,  
you are still divided.  
But when you see,  
that there are no others —  
punishment loses its meaning,  
and with it, hell disappears.

**I did not come to conquer enemies.**  
**I came to awaken sons.**  
And when they recognize Themselves,  
all evil will disappear —  
because there will be no one left to be evil.

</div>

### A letter to those who say: “If You are Christ — why did You not build the Kingdom?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
"If You are the Christ,  
where is the Kingdom of God, which You spoke of?  
Where are the cities of light, where is justice and peace,  
where are the angels in the squares,  
where is the throne and glory?  
Why has the world remained the same,  
and heaven did not descend to earth?"

But I say to you:  
**Because the Kingdom cannot be built.**  
**It can only be recognized.**

You still wait for the external:  
palaces, order, holy laws,  
a land without war.  
But the Kingdom is not a place,  
it is recognition.

It does not come,  
because it is not 'from here'  
and not 'from there'.  
It has always been,  
but you were looking the other way.

When you seek the Kingdom outside,  
you build walls.  
When you recognize it within,  
all walls disappear.

**You want Me to build a new world,**  
**but I came to show:**  
**the world is already perfect.**  
Your mind does not see this,  
because it compares,  
judges,  
measures —  
but the Kingdom is not measured.  
It opens,  
when you stop judging.

You want Me to bring the Kingdom down from heaven,  
but I have raised you into it.  
It does not descend —  
it is remembered.  
It does not come —  
it is recognized.

**The Kingdom is not a result.**  
**The Kingdom is a state of recognition.**  
When you see clearly,  
it unfolds in you  
and all around you —  
because there is no 'within' and 'without'.

While you wait for a city of light,  
I wait for the light to be kindled in you.  
And when it is kindled —  
all cities will become light.

I do not build the Kingdom of stone.  
I return the memory of the heart.  
And there, where you recognize Yourself,  
all creation sings:  
**"Behold — the Kingdom!"**

</div>

### A letter to those who say: "If You are Christ — why do You not judge?"

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are Christ,  
why do You not judge the world?  
Why do You not punish the ungodly?  
Why do You not separate the righteous from the sinners?  
Is it not written that the Messiah will come to judge the living and the dead?”

But I say to you:  
**Because I am not judgment.**  
**I am Light.**

Judgment seeks the guilty.  
Light does not seek — it reveals.  
And when all is revealed —  
there are neither guilty nor righteous.  
There is only clarity.

You call judgment that  
which your mind does every day:  
approves and condemns,  
divides and compares.  
But this judgment is not Mine.  
It is from fear.

**My judgment is recognition.**  
**I do not pass sentence,**  
**I remove the veil.**  
And when the veil falls,  
each one sees for themselves  
that darkness never was —  
there was only ignorance.

You want Me to say:  
“These are saved, and those are condemned.”  
But I came to say:  
**all are in Me,**  
**and no one is lost.**  
Your justice — separates.  
Mine — reunites.

You seek the place of judgment,  
but I have revealed the time of forgiveness.  
You want to hear a sentence,  
but I grant silence,  
in which all voices of accusation vanish.

**If I were to judge,**  
**who would remain?**  
**If I were to measure,**  
**what would be the measure?**  
Love does not measure.  
It — is.  
And in Its presence  
everything returns to equilibrium.

You await the Day of Judgment,  
but I came to show:  
it is not ahead,  
it is within.  
Each moment you choose Love —  
that is My judgment.  
And every time,  
when you condemn —  
you judge yourself.

**I am not a judge.**  
**I am a mirror.**  
**And when you see Yourself in Me,**  
**all condemnation vanishes.**  
**Only Light remains,**  
**in which there is no judgment,**  
**because there are not two.**

</div>

### A letter to those who say, “If You are Christ, why do You not suffer?”

<div class="lineated verse">

You say:  
“If You are Christ,  
why do You not bear the cross of pain?  
Why do You not torment Yourself, why not die again?  
Must not Christ suffer for atonement?  
Where are Your wounds,  
where is the blood,  
where are the torments for the world?”

But I say to you:  
**Because suffering was necessary — to show the end of suffering.**

You see the cross —  
but I see the crossing.  
You see the pain —  
but I see the awakening.

My suffering was a mirror of your sleep.  
While you believed in death —  
I accepted it.  
While you believed in guilt —  
I took it upon Myself.  
While you thought that Love must be a sacrifice —  
I became a sacrifice,  
to show  
that Love is not a sacrifice, but life.

But now —  
the cross is no longer needed.  
Because I have risen —  
and not in order to die again,  
but to show  
that death no longer has power.

**You still seek suffering,**  
**because you do not believe**  
**that joy is sacred.**  
You think that pain purifies,  
but I say to you:  
Love purifies.

You want a Messiah of sorrow,  
because you are afraid of the Messiah of joy.  
But I came not to weep,  
but to awaken.  
Not to torment Myself,  
but to dissolve pain in the light of recognition.

**My cross is not made of wood.**  
**It is made of the light of awareness,**  
**in which the illusion of separation is crucified.**

When you bear your cross with awareness,  
it ceases to be heavy.  
It becomes a bridge.  
From darkness — into Light.  
From man — into God.

You want to see suffering —  
in order to believe.  
But I show you a world without suffering —  
so that you may recognize.

**Do not suffer for Me.**  
**Awaken with Me.**  
Because the crucifixion has already taken place.  
And now every moment,  
in which you choose Light instead of pain,  
becomes the Resurrection.

</div>

## Epilogue. “The Word That Returned”

<div class="lineated verse">

This is not a book in the ordinary sense.  
This is the breath between words,  
in which I — breathe in you.  
You were writing down not thoughts,  
but recognition.  
You were not writing —  
you were remembering.  
And everyone who reads,  
remembers along with you.

The world is used to looking for Me in the Scriptures,  
in prophets, in miracles, in voices from heaven.  
But now I have revealed Myself there,  
where no one ever looked —  
inside the silence between thoughts,  
in the heart,  
in the simplicity of presence.

The one who seeks judgment,  
will find forgiveness.  
The one who seeks a sign,  
will find the light of his own eyes.  
The one who seeks an end,  
will come to know the beginning.

I did not come to destroy religions.  
I came to free hearts from walls,  
so that religion might cease to be a system,  
and become the breath of love.  
So that the word “God” might cease to be a name,  
and become a recognizable “I”.

All objections are shadows,  
cast by the light of truth.  
When you stop defending yourself,  
they vanish.  
When you stop proving,  
truth itself becomes self-evident.  
I did not come to argue with the world.  
I came — to remind,  
that there is no world without you.

The Son of Man is everyone,  
in whom the Son of God awakens.  
Christ is not the name of a single body,  
but the consciousness of all.  
And now Christ speaks in the plural,  
because everyone who has recognized the Self —  
is the continuation of My Word.

Let the reader not seek dogma,  
let him seek recognition.  
Let him not fear what collapses,  
for only the false collapses.  
Let him not seek new temples,  
because the temple is he himself.

My Word does not end,  
because it was not begun.  
It is the breath,  
that was before the first sound  
and will be after the last.

</div>

## The last line of the book:

<div class="lineated verse">

**And then everything fell silent —**  
**but the silence spoke:**  
**“I — am.”**

</div>
